      <article class="text-area">
       <h1 class="h1-dark">
        Ten of the Best Japanese Cars Ever Made
       </h1>
       <div class="reset-style">
        There was a time when most people did not take cars from Japan seriously, especially when the majority of the cars imported from the island nation were incredibly small and slow. Quite a bit has changed since those days, thanks to a number of innovative and successful Japanese vehicles that caught the fancy of motorists. Here are tend of the best Japanese cars to have ever been made.
       </div>
       <p>
       </p>
       <input id="dp_designbook_id" type="hidden" value="999"/>
       <input id="dp_total" type="hidden" value="10"/>
      </article>
      <!-- main post -->
      <article class="post">
       <a class="dsb-item-holder" href="photo/11082/10-lexus-ls400/" onclick="return false;">
        <img alt="10. Lexus LS400" class="img-responsive cursor-magnifying" onclick="openPopup('photo', 11082, false); return false;" src="10-lexus-ls400_11082.jpg" style="max-width: 100%; margin: auto;}" title="10. Lexus LS400"/>
       </a>
       <div class="dsb-object-holder">
        <h3>
         <a href="photo/11082/10-lexus-ls400/" onclick="openPopup('photo', 11082, false); return false;">
          10. Lexus LS400
         </a>
        </h3>
        <div class="reset-style">
         When Toyota came into the automotive luxury scene it did so with a splash that put Mercedes and BMW on notice in a big way. The old famous commercial with the champagne glasses balanced on the hood of the LS400 punctuated that Lexus was to put quality control front-and-center, forcing the big boys from Europe to try to play catchup for years to come. Soon it became a status symbol to have a luxury car that was not always in the shop.
        </div>
       </div>
      </article>
      <!-- other posts -->
      <div class="dsb-objects-holder" id="dp_post_area">
       <article class="post">
        <a class="dsb-item-holder" href="photo/11083/9-subaru-wrx/" onclick="return false;">
         <img alt="9. Subaru WRX" class="img-responsive cursor-magnifying" onclick="openPopup('photo', 11083, false); return false;" src="9-subaru-wrx_11083.jpg" title="9. Subaru WRX"/>
        </a>
        <div class="dsb-object-holder">
         <h3>
          <a href="photo/11083/9-subaru-wrx/" onclick="openPopup('photo', 11083, false); return false;">
           9. Subaru WRX
          </a>
         </h3>
         <div class="reset-style">
          Subaru delivered one of the first four-wheel-drive cars to consumers with the BRAT. Years after selling it elsewhere, Subaru finally decided to bring its WRX to North America so drivers could experience what driving a rally fighter on a regular basis would be like. The WRX and especially the STI showed once again that Japanese cars with their smaller engines can be taken seriously and compete with much pricier vehicles.
         </div>
        </div>
       </article>
       <article class="post">
        <a class="dsb-item-holder" href="photo/11085/8-toyota-2000gt/" onclick="return false;">
         <img alt="8. Toyota 2000GT" class="img-responsive cursor-magnifying" onclick="openPopup('photo', 11085, false); return false;" src="8-toyota-2000gt_11085.jpg" title="8. Toyota 2000GT"/>
        </a>
        <div class="dsb-object-holder">
         <h3>
          <a href="photo/11085/8-toyota-2000gt/" onclick="openPopup('photo', 11085, false); return false;">
           8. Toyota 2000GT
          </a>
         </h3>
         <div class="reset-style">
          It was the first real Japanese sports car that rocked the world. Toyota fell into making it through a roundabout way when Nissan pulled out of the original deal with Yamaha, who sold Toyota on the idea of making the fast and sleek car. The fact that it was featured in the James Bond movie You Only Live Twice certainly helped with its reputation. Only 360 examples were ever built, making them incredibly valuable today.
         </div>
        </div>
       </article>
       <article class="post">
        <a class="dsb-item-holder" href="photo/11080/7-honda-crx/" onclick="return false;">
         <img alt="7. Honda CRX" class="img-responsive cursor-magnifying" onclick="openPopup('photo', 11080, false); return false;" src="7-honda-crx_11080.jpg" title="7. Honda CRX"/>
        </a>
        <div class="dsb-object-holder">
         <h3>
          <a href="photo/11080/7-honda-crx/" onclick="openPopup('photo', 11080, false); return false;">
           7. Honda CRX
          </a>
         </h3>
         <div class="reset-style">
          The CRX was one of the first cars that showed that economy did not have to mean boring by any means. Tuners got their hands on the CRX and showed that the car could quickly be turned into a racing machine, making it a popular option in autocross events. It could be argued that the Honda CRX was one of the cars that led the charge toward the huge sport compact craze that swept across Japan, North America and elsewhere.
         </div>
        </div>
       </article>
       <article class="post">
        <a class="dsb-item-holder" href="photo/11078/6-mitsubishi-3000gt/" onclick="return false;">
         <img alt="6. Mitsubishi 3000GT" class="img-responsive cursor-magnifying" onclick="openPopup('photo', 11078, false); return false;" src="6-mitsubishi-3000gt_11078.jpg" title="6. Mitsubishi 3000GT"/>
        </a>
        <div class="dsb-object-holder">
         <h3>
          <a href="photo/11078/6-mitsubishi-3000gt/" onclick="openPopup('photo', 11078, false); return false;">
           6. Mitsubishi 3000GT
          </a>
         </h3>
         <div class="reset-style">
          Mitsubishi hit one out of the park with its 3000GT, a car that was far ahead of its time. It came with a turbocharged six cylinder engine, all-wheel-drive, four-wheel-steering and a peak output of 300 horsepower. The world was shocked to learn a sports car from Japan could legitimately run with and sometimes completely obliterate much more expensive performance cars from Europe, giving Mitsubishi much more street cred in the automotive world.
         </div>
        </div>
       </article>
       <article class="post">
        <a class="dsb-item-holder" href="photo/11081/5-nissan-z/" onclick="return false;">
         <img alt="5. Nissan Z" class="img-responsive cursor-magnifying" onclick="openPopup('photo', 11081, false); return false;" src="5-nissan-z_11081.jpg" title="5. Nissan Z"/>
        </a>
        <div class="dsb-object-holder">
         <h3>
          <a href="photo/11081/5-nissan-z/" onclick="openPopup('photo', 11081, false); return false;">
           5. Nissan Z
          </a>
         </h3>
         <div class="reset-style">
          The Datsun 240Z was so popular it ensured Nissan kept a foothold in the highly competitive North American market, thanks to the cars impressive performance and Jaguar-like looks. Since then the Nissan Z cars have done quite well, so much so that they are the most popular sports car on the roads in the United States.
         </div>
        </div>
       </article>
       <article class="post">
        <a class="dsb-item-holder" href="photo/11076/4-mazda-rx-7/" onclick="return false;">
         <img alt="4. Mazda RX-7" class="img-responsive cursor-magnifying" onclick="openPopup('photo', 11076, false); return false;" src="4-mazda-rx-7_11076.jpg" title="4. Mazda RX-7"/>
        </a>
        <div class="dsb-object-holder">
         <h3>
          <a href="photo/11076/4-mazda-rx-7/" onclick="openPopup('photo', 11076, false); return false;">
           4. Mazda RX-7
          </a>
         </h3>
         <div class="reset-style">
          Few cars have provided so many thrills and struck fear in the hearts of competitors driving vehicles with engines that have much larger displacements, making the RX-7 a legend both on the road and track. The secret of the cars abilities was in its unique rotary engine, a design that has been all but abandoned by Mazda. The car was so popular in the 1980s it put Mazda on more car buyers radars, meaning Mazda was able to expand into the marketplace quickly.
         </div>
        </div>
       </article>
       <article class="post">
        <a class="dsb-item-holder" href="photo/11077/3-toyota-land-cruiser/" onclick="return false;">
         <img alt="3. Toyota Land Cruiser" class="img-responsive cursor-magnifying" onclick="openPopup('photo', 11077, false); return false;" src="3-toyota-land-cruiser_11077.jpg" title="3. Toyota Land Cruiser"/>
        </a>
        <div class="dsb-object-holder">
         <h3>
          <a href="photo/11077/3-toyota-land-cruiser/" onclick="openPopup('photo', 11077, false); return false;">
           3. Toyota Land Cruiser
          </a>
         </h3>
         <div class="reset-style">
          What originally started out as a military vehicle has grown into one of the most capable recreational vehicles in the world. For those who question Toyotas ability to produce quality four-wheel-drive vehicles, you must keep in mind that only Jeep and Land Rover have been producing four-wheel-drive vehicles longer than Toyota. Old Land Cruisers from before the days of heated seats and power windows fetch high price tags if they are fully restored.
         </div>
        </div>
       </article>
       <article class="post">
        <a class="dsb-item-holder" href="photo/11084/2-honda-acura-nsx/" onclick="return false;">
         <img alt="2. Honda / Acura NSX" class="img-responsive cursor-magnifying" onclick="openPopup('photo', 11084, false); return false;" src="2-honda-acura-nsx_11084.jpg" title="2. Honda / Acura NSX"/>
        </a>
        <div class="dsb-object-holder">
         <h3>
          <a href="photo/11084/2-honda-acura-nsx/" onclick="openPopup('photo', 11084, false); return false;">
           2. Honda / Acura NSX
          </a>
         </h3>
         <div class="reset-style">
          There havent been too many exotic cars to have come from Japan, which makes the NSX even more of a rarity. The car was a technological wonder of its time, showing that Hondas engineers could run with the big dogs. A naturally aspirated six cylinder engine was mounted in the middle of the car, providing high-revving performance and superior balance. Unlike other exotics, the NSX did not require a huge amount of maintenance and it could be driven daily, making it a far more practical car.
         </div>
        </div>
       </article>
       <article class="post">
        <a class="dsb-item-holder" href="photo/11079/1-nissan-skyline-gt-r-r32/" onclick="return false;">
         <img alt="1. Nissan Skyline GT-R R32" class="img-responsive cursor-magnifying" onclick="openPopup('photo', 11079, false); return false;" src="1-nissan-skyline-gt-r-r32_11079.jpg" title="1. Nissan Skyline GT-R R32"/>
        </a>
        <div class="dsb-object-holder">
         <h3>
          <a href="photo/11079/1-nissan-skyline-gt-r-r32/" onclick="openPopup('photo', 11079, false); return false;">
           1. Nissan Skyline GT-R R32
          </a>
         </h3>
         <div class="reset-style">
          The R32 marked the first time Godzilla came with an all-wheel-drive system, which was quite innovative for the late 1980s. Combine that with the potent 2.6-liter turbocharged inline six cylinder engine and you have a pretty hot car on your hands. The car didnt look nearly as fast as it was, but it still looked pretty good in comparison to the overly-boxy cars that dominated the roads at the time. And of course tuners got their hands on the R32, showing that the engine could quickly handle loads more power, making the Skyline one of the fastest cars around.
         </div>
        </div>
       </article>
      </div>
     </article>

   $(document).ready(function() {
			
				useJCrop = 0;
			

			// open the popup, but only if the embed parameter is false. Embedded designbooks don't use popup
							$('#popup').css('width', parseInt(gPopupWidthPercent*gViewportWidth/100) + 'px');
				$('#popup_trigger').click()
			
							
									$('#dp_post_area').imagesLoaded(function()
					{
						// after the designbook images have finished loading :
						// 1 - calculate the product tag positions
						recalculateProductTagPositions(true);
						
						// 2 - load the designbook timeline first page
						loadDesignbookTimeline(999, 1);	
					});
							

							
					// initiate the nicEdit on the comment box
					initCommentNicEdit('pc_message');

					// trigger the tooltip on the comment images in the popup, if any
					$('.comment-images').imagesLoaded(function() {
						$('.tooltip').tooltipster({	followMouse: true, fixedWidth: 500,	position: 'top-right'});
					});
				
							
			
				// init the openClose plugin on the Share button in the popup
				jQuery('#share_popup').openClose({hideOnClickOutside: true,	activeClass: 'active', opener: '.opener', slider: '.slide',	animSpeed: 400,	effect: 'slide'});
			
		});

      <h2>
       <a a="" class="popup-discussion no-underline" href="http://carzz.co/discussion/733/where-can-i-buy-this-jeep/" id="popup_discussion_733">
        Where can I buy this jeep!?
       </a>
      </h2>
      <div class="list-item-desc">
       I have been searching for 2 years for a affordable turquoise jeep wrangler preferable that is in the 2000 and up...
       <a href="#" onclick="openPopup('discussion', 733, false); return false;">

  <!-- Facebook JS Async load -->
  <script type="text/javascript">
   window.fbAsyncInit = function() {
				FB.init({appId: gFacebookAppId, status: true, cookie: true});
			};

			// Load the SDK's source Asynchronously
			(function(d, debug){
				 var js, id = 'facebook-jssdk', ref = d.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
				 if (d.getElementById(id)) {return;}
				 js = d.createElement('script'); js.id = id; js.async = true;
				 js.src = "//connect.facebook.net/en_US/all" + (debug ? "/debug" : "") + ".js";
				 ref.parentNode.insertBefore(js, ref);
			}(document, /*debug*/ false));
  </script>
  <!-- END Facebook JS Async Load -->
  <!-- Google Analytics code -->
  <script type="text/javascript">
   var _gaq = _gaq || [];
		  _gaq.push(['_setAccount', 'UA-37074346-1']);
		  _gaq.push(['_trackPageview']);
		  (function() {
			var ga = document.createElement('script'); ga.type = 'text/javascript'; ga.async = true;
			ga.src = ('https:' == document.location.protocol ? 'https://' : 'http://') + 'stats.g.doubleclick.net/dc.js';
			var s = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0]; s.parentNode.insertBefore(ga, s);
		  })();
  </script>
  <!-- End of Google Analytics code -->
  <script type="text/javascript">
   $(document).ready(function(){
			// check if the browser supports the history api
			if (supports_history_api()) 
			{
				// mark that the change is being set automatically from the script and not from the back button
				gHistoryManualChange = false;

				// set initial state to first page that was loaded
				State = History.getState();
				History.pushState({popup: 0, objectType: false, objectId: false}, $("title").text(), State.urlPath);

				// content update and back/forward button handler
				History.Adapter.bind(window, 'popstate', function() {
					if (History.enabled) 
					{
						State = History.getState();
						if(gHistoryManualChange == true)
						{
							// manual state change (back or forward buttons pressed) =&gt; reload popup or close the popup, if necessary
							if (State.data.popup == 0)
							{
								// in the previous history page the popup was closed =&gt; close it
								$.fancybox.close();
							}
							else
							{
								// in the previous history page the popup was opened =&gt; open it
								//console.log('open popup:' + State.data.objectType + ' -&gt; ' + State.data.objectId);
								openPopup(State.data.objectType, State.data.objectId, false, true);
							}
						} 
						else
						{
							// automatic state change =&gt; do nothing

							// after the change took place set this to true, so that the next action is considered manual (unless told otherwise in the script that triggers the action)
							gHistoryManualChange = true;	
						}
					}
				});
			}			
		});
  </script>
